msg:After staying for three nights, I found some problems, but overall it was not bad. If I have the opportunity to go again, I will continue to choose this hotel to stay!

Location: Next to Central Avenue, it is a 2-3 minute walk. There are parking spaces at the door, but it is not recommended to let the car in, it is easy to get stuck in traffic and it is difficult to turn around.

Environment: The front desk is on the right hand side of the door, which is small. Next to it is the book bar, which is the breakfast dining area. The space is not large, and you need to wait for a seat during the breakfast peak.

Breakfast: It is divided into ordering + buffet. The ordering is divided into Chinese and Western, with two dishes in each category. If it is not enough, you can add more. There are not many types of buffet. The hotel is next to the red brick morning market, so it is okay not to choose hotel breakfast.

Hygiene: It‚Äôs okay, but there are "little surprises" in the linens, such as hair, and the coffee cup will also have lipstick marks left by the previous user. Train them well!

Service: The only two comfortable staff members are Lin Jing at the front desk. Every time I see her, she is super enthusiastic, helping to communicate matters, and warm and thoughtful; the other is the fat man with a belly at the door (sorry I forgot his name). Every time I go in and out, this gentleman will greet me very warmly, especially when I go out in the morning. Hearing such a greeting will make me feel very good all day‚ù§Ô∏è
Other people have service awareness, but they are also generous and straightforward like northerners. They are comfortable to get along with, but they are not very professional in the hotel service industry.

Afternoon tea at the Spring Book Bar for Two: It is available every day. You can go directly to the front desk area to pick it up, and you can also take it to the room to eat.

Junyi souvenirs: You have to go to the front desk to pick it up. If you forget, it will be gone, for example, I forgot.

msg:I stayed in two hotels in Harbin this time. This is the second one. It is the best hotel I have ever stayed in. There is no other. I will stay here next time I come to Harbin.
Hotel location: Turn right and walk 200 meters to the center of Central Street. Turn left and walk 100 meters to the Hongzhuan Morning Market. It is also very convenient to take a taxi to other attractions.
Service: After staying in so many five-star hotels, Junyi has the most thoughtful service. Every service staff is warm and polite. When waiting for check-in, the waiter first delivers hot towels and hot tea to relieve the fatigue of the journey. The handsome guy delivered the luggage directly to the room and introduced various facilities in detail. My son said, I have nothing to ask. This uncle introduced it too comprehensively. I booked a double breakfast room. After arriving at the hotel, I found that it was too close to the Hongzhuan Morning Market, so I wanted to cancel the hotel breakfast. The hotel actively cooperated with Ctrip to help me with the procedures. Ctrip was also very awesome. The breakfast refund was credited in seconds. Afternoon tea is from 10 am to 10 pm. Although there are not too many varieties, there are freshly ground coffee, hot tea, fruit salad, fruit and biscuits. They can also be delivered to the room. The waiters also pay attention to the status of the guests at any time and provide services in time. We were given exquisitely packaged souvenirs when we checked out. Several waiters kept sending us to the car. The driver who picked us up at the airport said that he thought we were friends with him because of his thoughtfulness. üòÅ
Room: The room is moderate in size and very clean. There is a small garden downstairs where you can drink tea. The room on the first floor has a small yard.
Dining: The two streets before and after the hotel are restaurants frequented by nearby residents. They are delicious and inexpensive, much better than the restaurants on Central Avenue.

msg:First impression of staying at this hotel for the first time

Service: The elevator was under maintenance on the day I checked in, so I might need to take the stairs. The room was upgraded for me, which was a very good experience.

Breakfast disadvantages: Breakfast is actually pretty good, divided into Western and Chinese set meals, leaving some very small buffets. If you rush for the early bus in the morning, the food service will be very slow. Moreover, the disadvantage of this seemingly customized service is that the guest time is not controllable. When there are more people, many things are easily lacking, and you can only order one breakfast set. Not as convenient as self-service at all. If you're not full, go out and eat another one. The eating experience is not as good as a fully self-service one. The breakfast time is also unreasonable. Guests who take the early bus cannot have breakfast. The accommodation fee includes breakfast, which will leave a gap.
Hotel environment: It is very close to Central Street and only 12 minutes from Harbin Station. The transportation is quite convenient, but the road there with luggage is very crowded. The basic buildings are still full. There is still a gap between online pictures and real on-site effects. There is a small amount of passing traffic at the hotel entrance, which is a bit noisy. The hotel is still small, there is no swimming pool, and there is only one elevator, so if there is a large flow of people, you still need to wait.

Service attitude: It's commendable, but it doesn't make people feel like there is butler service, which is commendable. But it doesn't feel like it's up to five-star hotel standards. Of course, the price is there and I don't ask for much.

To sum up, I feel average and may not want to stay here. In addition to being closer to Central Street and the morning market. Nothing else. close

Facilities: The room we stayed in was very spacious and the supporting facilities were quite complete. Advantages ‚úî There is a door blocker next to the door of the room. When you open the door, you can only push it open a crack. This is really considerate for girls traveling! The toilet is a smart toilet, and the seat cushion will be warm and very comfortable. The room is also equipped with a capsule coffee machine, which is really a surprise! For those who like to drink coffee, it is much better than providing a small bag of instant coffee! Disadvantages ‚úòThe shower room is really disappointing. First of all, the hand shower üöø cannot be fixed at all and can only spray water against the wall. If you use a top spray, the water will be very dispersed and the water flow will be small (maybe the nozzle is blocked or the water pressure is not enough). For girls with long hair, washing your hair once is too strenuous. I strongly recommend improvement! There is also the retractable makeup mirror next to the sink. It has its own halo, which is a plus. However, I don‚Äôt know whether it is due to time or poor contact. The mirror in our house only lights up at a certain angle (but this angle is also No one can be illuminated -_-||), I am completely speechless
Overall, the hotel has a strategic location, the service staff are very welcoming, and the rooms are clean and spacious. I hope the hotel can improve the issues raised. It is still worth recommending to friends who are traveling or on business.
